2073 <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words

2074 " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">

2075Have you heard of the new TikTok trend called, “Skin Cycling?” Skin cycling is a regimen that alternates between using active ingredients and letting the skin rest. Typically, it’s a four-night routine. However, according to Dr. Kseniya Kobets, Board-certified Dermatologist and Director of Cosmetic Dermatology at Montefiore Einstein Advanced Care—Westchester, if you have sensitive skin, you can still skin cycle, but you should approach exfoliation with caution. Dr. Kobets says, “Exfoliating with a physical exfoliant makes sensitive skin more at risk for irritation or allergic reaction, especially if you’re just starting out with exfoliants or retinoids.”

2076

2077Learn more: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/gcU9xPtG?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>

2078https://lnkd.in/gcU9xPtG</a>

3523 <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words

3524 " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">

3525Montefiore Einstein nursing was highlighted for their incredible work during the New York Organization for Nursing Leadership’s (NYONL) 31st Annual Meeting and Leadership Conference in Tarrytown, NY. Montefiore Einstein’s Elodia Mercier, MS, RN-C, BS, NE, Director of Nursing Throughput Operations; Mohamed Yasin, MSN, MPH, RN, NE-BC, Administrative Nurse Manager; and Obiageli Ubakanma, MBA, RN, BSN, WCC, Administrative Nurse Manager, presented an impressive poster on the Moses Discharge Lounge which has saved 10,000+ bed hours, significantly enhanced patient satisfaction, and has seen six times the number of patients on average as compared to other hospital lounges. Congratulations to all!

4002The 2020 Focused Asthma Updates introduced a paradigm shift in the treatment of asthma that includes symptom-based adjustments to outpatient asthma treatment that vary by age and severity. The length and complexity of the updates have made them challenging to adopt. Montefiore Einstein’s Karen L. Warman, MD, Pediatrician at Children’s Hospital at Montefiore (CHAM), hopes that an increase in the national adoption of “SMART '' and “START” therapy will help improve pediatric asthma management. Learn more in her article “Get SMART: Teaching Pediatric Residents the 2020 Focused Asthma Updates' Recommendations for Symptom-Based Medication Increases,” published in the Journal of Teaching and Learning Resources (Association of American Medical Colleges): <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/eMEkQfmw?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>

4003https://lnkd.in/eMEkQfmw</a>

4468 <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words

4469 " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">

4470Could you be allergic to your lipstick? Some common culprits in lipsticks include metals like nickel, dyes, perfumes, and fragrance mixes that could cause allergic reactions explains Dr. Kseniya Kobets, Board-certified Dermatologist and Director of Cosmetic Dermatology at Montefiore Einstein Advanced Care—Westchester. She says, “Ironically, people can also be allergic to ingredients that are supposed to hydrate the lips, like lanolin and propolis.”

4471

4940 <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words

4941 " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">

4942Dr. Lauren Gluck, Assistant Professor of Neurology and Director of the Montefiore Multiple Sclerosis Center, provides insights into the challenges of shared decision-making (SDM) in managing multiple sclerosis (MS). For Neurology Live, Dr. Gluck highlights involving patients in treatment choices and the positive impact of SDM on patient empowerment, and emphasizes the need for data-driven insights to enhance MS management.

4943

5883 <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words

5884 " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">

5885On August 22, the U.S. Food and Drug Administration (FDA) approved the first Respiratory Syncytial Virus (RSV) vaccine for pregnant people. Montefiore Einstein’s Dr. Betsy C. Herold, Chief, Division of Pediatric Infectious Disease, Children’s Hospital at Montefiore, highlights the impact this will have on children, their optimal use and potential challenges.
